       <article class="content-wrapper wrapper clearfix detail-block-md" id="article-37765">
        <header class="content-header">
         <h1>
          Womans Parents Accepting Of Mixed-Attractiveness Relationship
         </h1>
        </header>
        <main class="content-body large-thing" data-area="Article Body">
         <div class="content-masthead">
          <figure class="content-image on-trigger-overlay">
           <div class="image" data-image-id="28393" data-type="image">
            <div>
            </div>
            <noscript>
             <img src="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2839/3/16x9/600.jpg"/>
            </noscript>
           </div>
          </figure>
          <div class="on-overlay on-overlay-scale">
           <button class="on-overlay-close" type="button">
            Close
           </button>
           <figure class="content-image">
            <div class="image" data-image-id="28393" data-type="image">
             <div>
             </div>
             <noscript>
              <img src="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2839/3/16x9/600.jpg"/>
             </noscript>
            </div>
           </figure>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="content-meta small-thing">
          <div>
           <a class="content-type" data-track-action="Meta: Feature Type" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/search?tags=" href="/features/news-in-brief">
            NEWS IN BRIEF
           </a>
           <span class="content-published">
            January 14, 2015
           </span>
          </div>
          <div>
           <span class="content-issue">
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Issue" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/issue/5102/" href="/issue/5102/">
             Vol 51 Issue 02
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="content-tags">
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/dating" href="/tag/dating">
             Dating
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/parents" href="/tag/parents">
             Parents
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/lifestyle" href="/tag/lifestyle">
             Lifestyle
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <div class="article-share-tools share-container">
           <div class="share-tools share-widget" data-share-description="CHICAGOAdmitting it took them some time to come around to the idea, the parents of local woman Laura Stevens said Wednesday that they had finally accepted their daughters mixed-attractiveness relationship with Kyle Baker, a man who is consid..." data-share-image="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2839/3/16x9/1200.jpg" data-share-redirect-url="http://www.theonion.com/fb-close" data-share-title="Womans Parents Accepting Of Mixed-Attractiveness Relationship" data-share-url="http://www.theonion.com/r/37765">
            <a class="share-facebook button" data-action="Facebook share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Facebook" href="#" target="_blank" title="Share via Facebook">
             <i class="fa fa-facebook fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
            <a class="share-twitter button" data-action="Twitter share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Twitter" href="#" title="Share via Twitter">
             <i class="fa fa-twitter fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
            <a class="share-mail button" data-action="Email share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Email" href="#" title="Share via Email">
             <i class="fa fa-envelope fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="dfp dfp-slot-article-button" data-ad-unit="article-button" data-targeting='{"dfp_pagetype": "article", "dfp_content_id": 37765}'>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="large-thing content-main">
          <div class="content-text">
           <div>
            <p>
             CHICAGOAdmitting it took them some time to come around to the idea, the parents of local woman Laura Stevens said Wednesday that they had finally accepted their daughters mixed-attractiveness relationship with Kyle Baker, a man who is considerably worse-looking than she is. To be honest, we were quite surprised when Laura brought Kyle to the house for the first time, but eventually we came around to it, said Stevens mother, Janet, who noted that the pair were still met with uncomfortable stares and disapproval from other family membersespecially Lauras grandmotherat last years Thanksgiving dinner. Her father was particularly upset at first, but now I think hes learned to accept it, and hes even grown to like Kyle. Besides, Kyle seems to make Laura happy, and thats all that really matters. Janet Stevens went on to say that, if the two ever got married, she would love their children no matter how average-looking they are.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
